***кроить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кроить.html>крои́ть</a> (28673)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krojìti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кроить.html>крои́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kroítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскроить.html>раскрои́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скроить.html>скрои́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cut out (fabric to specific lengths and shapes to make clothes)</li></ol>

<p><b>кро<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>и́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крольчиха.html>крольчи́ха</a> (22490)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">крольк-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krolʹk-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, using the stem form found in e.g. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крольчонок.html>крольчо́нок</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krolʹčónok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крольчиха.html>крольчи́ха</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krolʹčíxa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крольчиха.html>крольчи́хи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крольчиха.html>крольчи́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крольчиха.html>крольчи́х</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кролик.html>кро́лик</a></b>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кроме.html>кро́ме</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">króme</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́шный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-éšnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кромешный.html>кроме́шный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kroméšnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>pitch-black, impenetrable <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">darkness</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тьма.html>тьма</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кромешный.html>кроме́шная</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tʹma <b>kroméšnaja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">total darkness</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>sheer, absolute, utter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ад.html>ад</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кромешный.html>кроме́шный</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ad <b>kroméšnyj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">sheer hell</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***крона.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крона.html>кро́на</a> (8110)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крона.html>кро́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">króna</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крона.html>кро́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крона.html>кро́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крона.html>кро́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>crown (of a tree)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">numismatics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> crown, koruna, krona, krone, kroon, króna</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>кро́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кропота́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kropotátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grumble; to fuss, to bustle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ли́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***кроткий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кроткий.html>кро́ткий</a> (11886)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">кротъкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krotŭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krotъkъ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">кро̀так</i> / <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">kròtak</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кроткий.html>кро́ткий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krótkij</span>) (<i>rare/awkward comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)кро́тче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gentle, meek, mild</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кротость.html>кро́тость</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">krótostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укрощать.html>укроща́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ukroščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">укрощение</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ukroščenije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крот.html>кро́т</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кий.html>кий</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3*a/c.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-кротк-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***кротость.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кротость.html>кро́тость</a> (21677)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:кротость.html>кро́тость</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krotostĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krotostь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кротость.html>кро́тость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krótostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кротость.html>кро́тости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кротость.html>кро́тости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кротость.html>кро́тостей</a></b>)

***кроха.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кроха.html>кро́ха</a> (15017)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">кръха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krŭxa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crumb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krъxa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кроха.html>кро́ха</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">króxa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кроха.html>кро́хи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кроха.html>кро́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кроха.html>кро́х</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крошка.html>кро́шка</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>crumb</li>
<li>little child</li></ol>

<p><b>кро́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ха.html>ха</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> согласовываться <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>частя́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>ре́чи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́го</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нского</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>рода</a>), 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-крох-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>.

***крохотный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крохотный.html>кро́хотный</a> (4038)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">кръхътьнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krŭxŭtĭnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">кръхъть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krŭxŭtĭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crumb, speck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krъxa</i>. See <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кроха.html>кро́ха</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">króxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крохотный.html>кро́хотный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">króxotnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>very small, tiny, minute
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крохотный.html>кро́хотная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>króxotnaja</b> kvartíra</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a tiny apartment</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кухня.html>ку́хня</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:крохотный.html>кро́хотная</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kúxnja <b>króxotnaja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">a tiny kitchen</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>кро́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:хота.html>хо́т</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крошево.html>кро́шево</a> (21482)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крошево.html>кро́шево</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">króševo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крошево.html>кро́шева</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крошево.html>кро́шева</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крошево.html>кро́шев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hash <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">chopped food, especially meat and potatoes</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

***крошить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крошить.html>кроши́ть</a> (15162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крошить.html>кроши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krošítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">покроши́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накрошить.html>накроши́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">искроши́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cut into small pieces, to chop, to crumble</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hack to pieces</li>
<li>to drop something like breadcrumbs on the ground</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крошка.html>кро́шка</a> (5874)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кроха.html>кро́ха</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">króxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крошка.html>кро́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">króška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крошка.html>кро́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крошка.html>кро́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крошка.html>кро́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>crumb, bit (small piece of biscuit, cookie, cake, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кроха.html>кро́ха</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">króxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: baby, little one</li></ol>

***круг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круг</a> (901)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krǫgъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krug</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>кру́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круги́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круго́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>circle, ring</li>
<li>sphere, range</li>
<li>orbit</li>
<li>average</li>
<li>slice</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">racing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lap</li></ol>
